<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:balken.html>balke</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*balco</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*balkô</i>.
</p>

***balkan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> balkan (19801)</h1><br></body> 
***balken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balken.html>balken</a> (19927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:balken.html>balken</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">belken</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bulken.html>bulken</a></i>, probably onomatopoeic. Similar formations are found in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">bölken</i> (from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span></span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:balk.html>balkje</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">belch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balken.html>balken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bray, make a donkey's sound</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to utter asinine talk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bawl, cry, weep loudly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a>, sing loudly</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huilebalk.html>huilebalk</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balk.html>balk</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ballen.html>ballen</a> (1444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ballen.html>ballen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play with a ball</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to form into a ball or similar shape; to clasp, clench (into a fist)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fuck</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ballen.html>ballen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***balling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balling.html>balling</a> (58127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ballinc</i>, assimilated from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">banlinc</i>, which consists of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ban</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-linc</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banneling.html>banneling</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balling.html>balling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ballingen.html>ballingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balling.html>ballinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>exile (exiled person)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bananenboot.html>bananenboot</a> (95553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banaan.html>banaan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">banana</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bananenboot.html>bananenboot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bananenboten.html>bananenboten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bananenboot.html>bananenbootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A banana boat, a boat that transports <a href = vnd.unilang:bananas.html>bananas</a>.</li>
<li>A banana boat, a yellow inflatable boat.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a> consisting of one or two <a href = vnd.unilang:bananas.html>bananas</a>, ice cream, whipped cream and often including chocolate, vaguely shaped like a boat.</li></ol>
</body>

***band.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> (956)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bant.html>bant</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. </p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bandiet.html>bandiet</a> (8320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">bandito</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bandstand.html>bandstand</a> (35338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Greenwich_Park_bandstand_Oct_07.jpg/220px-Greenwich_Park_bandstand_Oct_07.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Greenwich_Park_bandstand_Oct_07.jpg/330px-Greenwich_Park_bandstand_Oct_07.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Greenwich_Park_bandstand_Oct_07.jpg/440px-Greenwich_Park_bandstand_Oct_07.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2272" data-file-height="1704" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A traditional <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandstand.html>bandstand</a></b> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greenwich_Park" class="extiw" title="w:Greenwich Park">Greenwich Park</a>, London</div></div></div>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stand</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bandstand.html>bandstand</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bandstands</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small, open-air platform or enclosure for <a href = vnd.unilang:bands.html>bands</a> to play on, usually roofed.</li>
<li>A small, informal stage, usually located in nightclubs, where local and amateur musicians perform.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> rotunda</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandstand.html>bandstand</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speelt.html>speelt</a></li></ol>

***bandy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a> (36329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bander</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a> at tennis</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i>-y</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i> added due to influence from Spanish and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">bandear</i> and or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">bandir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the same root as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></i>. Compare also with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">banter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">bandies</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bandying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bandied</b>).
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To give and receive reciprocally; to exchange.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> (with somebody)</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To use or pass about casually.
<dl><dd><i>to have one's name <b>bandied</b> about (or around)</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1741</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Watts" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Isaac Watts">Isaac Watts</a>, <i>The Improvement of the Mind</i>, London: James Brackstone, Chapter 13, Section 20.3, p. 187,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/suppimproveofmin00wattuoft">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Let not obvious and known Truths, or some of the most plain and certain Propositions be <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a>’d</b> about in a Disputation, for a <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> Trial of Skill <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1928</b>,  Lawrence <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:bourne.html>Bourne</a>,  chapter 4, in  <cite>Well Tackled!</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5387037W">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Technical <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> like ferrite, perlite, graphite, and hardenite <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b>bandied</b> to and fro, and when Paget glibly <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> out such a <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> exotic as ferro-molybdenum, Benson <a href = vnd.unilang:forgot.html>forgot</a> that he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a master ship-builder, […]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To throw or strike reciprocally, like <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a> in sports.
<ul><li>c. <b>1605</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:King Lear">King Lear</a></i>, Act I, Scene 4,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=kinglearamp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Do you <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a> with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, you <a href = vnd.unilang:rascal.html>rascal</a>?</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1663</b>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hudibras" class="extiw" title="w:Hudibras">Hudibras</a></i>, by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Butler" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuel Butler">Samuel <a href = vnd.unilang:butler.html>Butler</a></a>, part 1, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Hudibras/Part_1/Canto_2" class="extiw" title="s:Hudibras/Part 1/Canto 2">canto 2</a>
<dl><dd>For as whipp'd <a href = vnd.unilang:tops.html>tops</a> and <b>bandied</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a>, / The learned hold, are animals; / So <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a> they affirm to be / <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>Mere</a> engines made by geometry <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1678</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ralph_Cudworth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ralph Cudworth"><a href = vnd.unilang:ralph.html>Ralph</a> Cudworth</a>, <i>The True Intellectual System of the Universe</i>, London: Richard Royston, Book I, Chapter 5, p. ,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A35345.0001.001">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>For, <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> no <i>Mastery</i> at all <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> our <i>Thoughts</i>, but they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> all like Tennis <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>Balls</a>, <b>Bandied</b>, and Struck upon us, as it <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> by <a href = vnd.unilang:rackets.html>Rackets</a> from without; then could <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> not steadily and constantly carry on any <i><a href = vnd.unilang:designs.html>Designs</a></i> and <i>Purposes</i> of Life.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fight (<i>with</i> or <i>against</i> someone).
<ul><li><b>1594</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Marlowe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Christopher Marlowe">Christopher Marlowe</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_II_(play)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edward II (play)">Edward II</a></i>, London: William Jones,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A07018.0001.001">[5]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Brother displaie my ensignes in the field,</dd>
<dd>Ile <b>bandie</b> with the <a href = vnd.unilang:barons.html>Barons</a> and the Earles,</dd>
<dd>And eyther <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a>, or liue with <i>Gaueston</i>.</dd></dl></li>
<li>c. <b>1594</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romeo_and_Juliet" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Romeo and Juliet"><a href = vnd.unilang:romeo.html>Romeo</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:juliet.html>Juliet</a></a></i>, Act III, Scene 1,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=romeojulietamp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[6]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Tybalt, Mercutio, the prince expressly hath</dd>
<dd>Forbidden <b>bandying</b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:verona.html>Verona</a> streets:</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1650</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Milton">John Milton</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eikonoklastes" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Eikonoklastes">Eikonoklastes</a></i>, London, Chapter 18, pp. 160-161,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A50898.0001.001">[7]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>But when a King setts himself to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></b> against the highest Court and residence of all his <a href = vnd.unilang:regal.html>Regal</a> power, he then, in the single person of a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:fights.html>fights</a> against his own Majesty and Kingship, and then indeed <a href = vnd.unilang:sets.html>sets</a> the first hand to his own deposing.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">bandier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">bandiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Bowlegged, or bending outward at the knees; as in <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bandy-legged</i>.
<ul><li><b>1794,</b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Blake" class="extiw" title="w:William Blake">William <a href = vnd.unilang:blake.html>Blake</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Little_Vagabond" class="extiw" title="s:The Little Vagabond">The Little Vagabond</a></i>, third stanza
<dl><dd>Then the <a href = vnd.unilang:parson.html>Parson</a> might preach, and <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>, and sing, / And <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>’d be as happy as <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> in the spring; / And modest <a href = vnd.unilang:dame.html>Dame</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>Lurch</a>, who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> always at church, / Would not have <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></b> children, nor fasting, nor birch.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1848</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Makepeace_Thackeray" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Makepeace Thackeray">William Makepeace Thackeray</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vanity_Fair_(novel)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vanity Fair (novel)">Vanity Fair</a></i>, Chapter 1:
<dl><dd>A black servant, who reposed on the box beside the fat coachman, uncurled his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> as soon as the <a href = vnd.unilang:equipage.html>equipage</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drew.html>drew</a> up opposite Miss Pinkerton's <a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a> brass plate, and as he pulled the bell at least a score of young heads <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> seen peering out of the narrow <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a> of the stately old brick house.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2004</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alan_Hollinghurst" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alan Hollinghurst">Alan Hollinghurst</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Line_of_Beauty" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Line of Beauty">The Line of Beauty</a></i>, Bloomsbury, 2005, Chapter 7,
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> drying near them, squat and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></b> and brown all <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, and <a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>Nick</a> remembered him from last year <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from the verb <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></i> in the sense "toss/bat back and forth",<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> or possibly from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> word <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">bando</i>, most likely derived from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bandją</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a curved stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/bandy" class="extiw" title="w:bandy"><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/bandy" class="extiw" title="w:bandy">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A winter sport played on ice, from which ice hockey developed.</li>
<li>A club <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> at the lower part for striking a ball at play; a hockey stick.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Johnson to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telugu_language" class="extiw" title="w:Telugu language">Telugu</a></span></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bandy.html>bandy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bandies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A carriage or cart used in India, especially one drawn by <a href = vnd.unilang:bullocks.html>bullocks</a>.</li></ol>
</body>

***banen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a> (4945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make way, to clear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baande.html>baande</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gras.html>gras</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>cleared</b> a path through the grass.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a> (240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">banghe</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">be-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">anghe</i>, the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an adverbial form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:enge.html>enge</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">narrow, confined</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:angst.html>angst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banger.html>banger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bangst.html>bangst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scared, frightened
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>Wees</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Please don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> be <b>afraid</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:donker.html>donker</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am <b>scared</b> of the dark!</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>fearful</li>
<li>anxious</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The adjective <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> accompanied with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i> (to be); for example: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></i> "I am afraid". Usage with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> (to have) also occurs <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> for example: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally proscribed.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bevreesd.html>bevreesd</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:angstig.html>angstig</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vruchtig</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verschrikt.html>verschrikt</a></span></li></ul>

***bannen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bannen.html>bannen</a> (26793)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bannen.html>bannen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bannan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bannaną</i>. The computational sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from, or at least strongly influenced by, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ban</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bannen.html>bannen</a></strong>
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ban (an IP address)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ban</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>harsh, tough <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">used mainly with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koude.html>koude</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omstandigheden.html>omstandigheden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">conditions</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
